			"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("WTCiraenSentinelBow_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.25*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.25*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 4 A_SetScale(0.2*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.2*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("WTCiraenSentinelBow_Shrink", 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_TRANSFERPOINTERS|SXF_TRANSFERSPECIAL|SXF_TRANSFERAMBUSHFLAG|SXF_SETMASTER,0,tid)
			TNT1 A 2
			TNT1 A 0 Thing_Remove(0)
			stop
		Death.ExpanderDMG:
		XDeath.ExpanderDMG:
			WH_7 M 0
			"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
			"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
			"####" "#" 0 A_PlaySound("duke/expand")
			Goto ExpanderLoop
		ExpanderLoop:
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(1.1*(user_scalex/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1))+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1)-CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",3)*2),1.1*(user_scaley/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scaley/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(ceilingz - (z + height + CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1) + 32) <= 0, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthY", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderDoubleX", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 40, "ExpanderPop")
			loop
		ExpanderPop:	
			"####" "#" 10
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ExpanderExplosion_Basic",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/explosion", 6, 1.0)
			TNT1 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("SamsaraDecorate",36,2)
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(96,2)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt", 1)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale (1.0, 1.0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetSolid
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeGibPopSpawner", 0, 0, height*2, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt",1)
			TNT1 A 1
			Stop
		Death.ExpanderDMGCoop:
		XDeath.ExpanderDMGCoop:
			WH_7 M 0
			"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
			"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
			"####" "#" 0 A_PlaySound("duke/expand")
			Goto ExpanderLoopCoop

			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(1.1*(user_scalex/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1))+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1)-CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",3)*2),1.1*(user_scaley/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scaley/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(ceilingz - (z + height + CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1) + 32) <= 0, 2)

			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(96,2)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt", 1)

			TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetSolid
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeGibPopSpawner", 0, 0, height*2, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt",1)
			TNT1 A 1
			Stop
	}

Actor WTBowArrow_Enemy : WTBowArrow { -NOEXTREMEDEATH +PIERCEARMOR Speed 110 Damage (random(4,6)*Random(2,1)) Obituary "%o was pierced by a ciraen slave." DamageType "" }

Actor WTCiraenSentinelFists : WitchavenEnemyBaseMelee {
   Tag "Ciraen Sentinel"
   Health 15
   Mass 1000
   PainChance 67
   Scale 0.365
   Speed 10	
   SeeSound ""
   ActiveSound ""
   PainSound "wtcsentinel/pain"
   DeathSound "wtcsentinel/die"
   +QUICKTORETALIATE
   Obituary "%o was killed by a ciraen slave."   
   States {
		Spawn:
			WH_7 M 0
			WH_7 M 1 A_JumpIfInventory("AlreadySpawned",1,"SpawnStandard")
			WH_7 M 1 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("ReMixerSpawnScript",0,1,0)
			WH_7 M 0 A_GiveInventory("AlreadySpawned",1)
		SpawnStandard:
			TNT1 A 0
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(128,"Spawn2")
		Spawn1:	
			WH_7 M 5 A_Look
			Loop
		Spawn2:
			WH_7 N 5 A_Look
			Loop
		Idle:
			TNT1 A 0 A_Look		
			WH_7 GG 3 A_Wander
			TNT1 A 0 A_Look
			WH_7 HH 3 A_Wander
			TNT1 A 0 A_Look			
			WH_7 II 3 A_Wander
			TNT1 A 0 A_Look			
			WH_7 JJ 3 A_Wander
			TNT1 A 0 A_Look			
			WH_7 KK 3 A_Wander
			TNT1 A 0 A_Look			
			WH_7 LL 3 A_Wander
			TNT1 A 0 A_Look			
			Loop   
		See:
			WH_7 GGHHIIJJKKLL 3 A_Chase("Melee","")
			Loop
		Melee:
			TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",0)
			WH_8 H 5 A_FaceTarget
			WH_8 I 6 A_CustomMeleeAttack(Random(5,15)/Random(2,1),"wtflesh/hit","wtflesh/punch")
			WH_8 J 5 A_FaceTarget
			WH_8 K 6 A_CustomMeleeAttack(Random(5,20)/Random(2,1),"wtflesh/hit","wtflesh/punch")
			Goto See
		Pain:
			WH_7 Y 4 A_Pain
			WH_7 Y 4
			Goto See
		Pain.MightyBoot:
			TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",1)
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySoundEx("duke/kickhit","body",0,0)

			TNT1 A 0 A_Recoil(14)
			WH_7 Y 16 A_Pain
			Goto See
		Pain.MarathonStun:
			TNT1 A 0 A_Stop
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("NothingSpeed")
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySoundEx("marathon/tech50/stun","body",0,0)
			WH_7 Y 5 A_FaceTarget
			TNT1 A 0 A_Gravity
			WH_7 Y 30 A_Pain
			WH_7 Y 70
			Goto See
		Death:
		XDeath:
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
			WH_7 O 4
			WH_7 P 4 A_Scream
			WH_7 Q 4 A_NoBlocking
			WH_7 R 4
			WH_7 STUVW 4
			WH_7 X -1 A_KillMaster
			Stop
		Raise:
			WH_7 X 5
			WH_7 WVUTSRQPO 5
			Goto See
		Death.TotenkopfFire:
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItem("Totenkopf_BurningGuard")
			TNT1 A 0 A_KillMaster
			TNT1 A 5 A_NoBlocking
			Stop			
		Death.RottFire:
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItem("BurningSkeleton")
			TNT1 A 0 A_KillMaster
			TNT1 A 0 A_NoBlocking		
			TNT1 A 5
		   Stop	
		Death.RottExplosive:
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("RottGibbedMan",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
			TNT1 A 1
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(128, 2)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("LudicrousGibsItem", 1)
			TNT1 A 0 A_KillMaster
			TNT1 A 5 A_NoBlocking
			Stop

actor WTCiraenSentinelFists_Shrink : WTCiraenSentinelFists
{
	+FRIGHTENED
	+NOTRIGGER
	-SHOOTABLE
	+THRUACTORS
	+NORADIUSDMG
	+VULNERABLE
	+QUICKTORETALIATE
	+COUNTKILL
	-NOGRAVITY
	+NODAMAGE
	+NOPAIN
	MaxStepHeight 0
	MaxDropOffHeight 0
	MeleeRange 16
	Height 16
	Health 1
	Speed 1
	PainChance "ShrinkDMG", 0

			WH_7 M 5 A_Look
			Loop
		See:

			"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(256, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfTargetInSideMeleeRange("DukeStomp")

			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("ChexClass", 1, 5) // this is supposed to be child friendly

	}

			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.7*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.7*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("WTCiraenSentinelBow_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)

			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.6*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.6*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("WTCiraenSentinelBow_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.55*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.55*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.5*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.5*(user_scaley/65536.0))

			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(0.3*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.3*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("WTCiraenSentinelBow_ShrinkEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)

			"####" "#" 4 A_SetScale(0.2*(user_scalex/65536.0),0.2*(user_scaley/65536.0))
			"####" "#" 0 A_SpawnItemEx("WTCiraenSentinelSpellAndStar_2_Shrink", 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_TRANSFERPOINTERS|SXF_TRANSFERSPECIAL|SXF_TRANSFERAMBUSHFLAG|SXF_SETMASTER,0,tid)

			TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN", 1)

			TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("SHOOTABLE", 0)
			Goto ShrunkLoop

			TNT1 A 1 A_KillMaster
			stop

		XDeath.ExpanderDMG:

			"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)

			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(ceilingz - (z + height + CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1) + 32) <= 0, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthY", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderDoubleX", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 40, "ExpanderPop")
			loop
		ExpanderPop:	
			"####" "#" 10
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ExpanderExplosion_Basic",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/explosion", 6, 1.0)
			TNT1 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("SamsaraDecorate",36,2)
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(96,2)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt", 1)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale (1.0, 1.0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetSolid
			TNT1 A 0 A_KillMaster
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeGibPopSpawner", 0, 0, height*2, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt",1)
			TNT1 A 1
			Stop
		Death.ExpanderDMGCoop:
		XDeath.ExpanderDMGCoop:
			WH_7 M 0
			"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scalex", scalex*65536.0)
			"####" "#" 0 A_SetUserVar("user_scaley", scaley*65536.0)
			"####" "#" 0 A_PlaySound("duke/expand")
			Goto ExpanderLoopCoop
		ExpanderLoopCoop:
			"####" "#" 1 A_SetScale(1.1*(user_scalex/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1))+((0.01*(user_scalex/65536.0))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1)-CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))*(CallACS("Samsara_Expander",3)*2),1.1*(user_scaley/65536.0)+((0.01*(user_scaley/65536.0))*CallACS("Samsara_Expander",2)))
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(ceilingz - (z + height + CallACS("Samsara_Expander",1) + 32) <= 0, 2)
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderGrowthY", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("ExpanderDoubleX", 1)
			"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIfInventory("ExpanderGrowthX", 40, "ExpanderPopCoop")
			loop
		ExpanderPopCoop:	
			"####" "#" 10
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ExpanderExplosion_Coop",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("duke/explosion", 6, 1.0)
			TNT1 A 1 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("SamsaraDecorate",36,2)
			TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteAlways("Samsara_KillCount", 0, 0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(96,2)
			TNT1 A 0 A_GiveToTarget("DukeGibTaunt", 1)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SetScale (1.0, 1.0)
			TNT1 A 0 A_UnsetSolid
			TNT1 A 0 A_KillMaster
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("UniversalBloodyHellGoreXDeathEffect",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DukeGibPopSpawner", 0, 0, height*2, 0, 0, 0, 0, SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_USEBLOODCOLOR)

			Stop
	}
